## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 100 page(s) - 100 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [label-title-only](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/label-title-only?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: Form elements should have a visible label

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<input type="text" name="q" id="buscador-header" maxlength="150" title="Buscar" placeholder="Buscar" class="ppg-search__input ppg-text ppg-text--lighted ppg-icon__search-ra" onfocus="javascript:this.value=''">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
#buscador-header
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('#buscador-header')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://administracion.gob.es/
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/centros-atencion-sociosanitaria
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/estancia-TSE
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/numeros-urgencia
- *...and 95 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 28 page(s) - 28 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [link-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: Links must have discernible text

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a target="_blank" href="https://europa.eu/youreurope/search/index_es.htm">
        	        <figure class="o-card__picture">
        		        <img alt="" title="" src="/dam/jcr:8505ed98-e821-4138-82c1-5b57e9cb3b99/your-europe.png">
        		    </figure>
    		    </a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.pseudopie_figure > a[target="_blank"]:nth-child(1)
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.pseudopie_figure > a[target="_blank"]:nth-child(1)')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:

#### Pattern 10: Affects 4 page(s) - 4 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor
**Issue**: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]
```

**How to Replicate**:

4. Run: `$x('ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]')`

**Impact**: minor
**Issue**: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide10">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://administracion.gob.es/
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/gl/index.html
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/va/index.html

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://administracion.gob.es/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]`

**Failure 2:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide01"]`

**Failure 3:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="2" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide02">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide02"]`

**Failure 4:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<a href="#tab-0" class="ppg-tabs__link ui-tabs-anchor" role="presentation" tabindex="-1" id="ui-id-1">Servicios ELECTRÓNICOS frecuentes</a>`
- XPath: `#ui-id-1`

**Failure 5:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide10">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"]`

#### Rule: [aria-input-field-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-input-field-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA input fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 20000px; transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);">`
- XPath: `.ppg-slick--type1 > .slick-list.draggable[aria-live="polite"] > .slick-track[role="listbox"]`

**Failure 2:**
- First identified: 2026-03-22
- Message: ARIA input fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 55000px; transform: translate3d(-600px, 0px, 0px);">`
- XPath: `div[data-fn="slick-type2"] > .slick-list.draggable[aria-live="polite"] > .slick-track[role="listbox"]`
